Travel Notes of Japan (13) 86

— Our Reporter, Hu Zhongchi, Hu Yizang

(8) Department Stores

On the day we visited the Osaka Mainichi Shimbun, we visited two large department stores in Osaka.

That morning, it rained heavily. When we walked out of the hotel, we saw the rain scene of this big city, which had a different kind of flavor. Most of the pedestrians on the street, men and women, were stepping on high wooden platforms and wearing paper umbrellas or cloth umbrellas. There were very few people wearing raincoats like us. All the tires of the cars were hung with rubber strips or palm brushes to prevent the mud and water on the road from splashing on the pedestrians when driving.

We have to go to the Hankyu Department Store near the hotel, we must cross the wide road in front of Osaka Station where vehicles are densely packed. It must be difficult to cross such a road when it is raining heavily, but Osaka's perfect traffic management system allows us to walk over without panic. There are very few traffic police on the streets of Osaka, and the traffic order is maintained entirely by machinery. The traffic lights on the road have three colors: red, green, and yellow, and they light up in turn by electrical automatic devices. There are also a series of large copper nails on the road marking the crosswalk. Pedestrians can wait for the green light to turn on and cross the road from the crosswalk. It doesn't matter if you are bolder and cross when the yellow light is on.

Entering the door of the Bankyu Department Store is a very large hall. Many people were walking back and forth there. From there, you can enter the Hanshin Elevated Railway Station. This train station will soon be connected to Osaka Station, which is tens of meters away. The underground passage project between the two is currently underway. We took the elevator in the hall and browsed everything in the various departments of the Hankyu Department Store. The scale of this department store seems to be much larger than Shanghai's Sincere and Wing On, but it does not have the hotels and amusement parks attached to Sincere and Wing On. The goods in each department have many patterns. It looks like more than 90% are domestic goods. To what extent Japan's industry has developed can be well understood from there. There is a painting exhibition hall, a mannequin display room, and a special sales market with a uniform price of ten cents and fifty cents. There is a photography studio where you can pick up the photos within an hour. The most noteworthy is the large canteen on the seventh floor.

This large canteen occupies the entire seventh floor of the building, selling Japanese, Chinese, and Western food at low prices. The very spacious hall is filled with large and small dining tables that can accommodate two or three thousand diners. Two rows of glass cabinets display various colorful foods and drinks, each labeled with its name and price. A cup of coffee costs only five cents. A Western Lunch (simple meal) costs only thirty cents. There are also several varieties of Chinese food, such as egg fried rice and Chinese noodles. The name "China Lunch" is the most peculiar. It is a large plate of mixed side dishes and a large bowl of white rice, priced at thirty cents. We walked into the cafeteria, it was lunch time. The cafeteria was packed with people. We searched for a long time before finding two empty seats next to a large table. Then a waitress came over, calculated the value of the drinks and food we wanted to order, and sent us to a female shopkeeper at the door counter to buy a few small food coupons (there are about ten kinds of food coupons, from five cents to fifty cents) because the rule there is to pay first and then eat. In a few minutes, the drinks and food we ordered were moved from the kitchen window to our front.

After lunch, we walked out of the Hankyu Department Store. After visiting the Mainichi Shimbun in the afternoon, we took the tram to Namba Shinchi in the southern district.

The tram fare in Osaka, like other major cities in Japan, adopts a uniform system. No matter how far or near, it is seven cents one way and fourteen cents round trip. The ticket sellers on the tram are all women, and they provide very attentive service to passengers. At each stop, they shout the name of the station and ask those who want to get off to get off. After the car starts, they report that the next station is something and ask those who want to get off to prepare in advance. When passengers get off, the ticket seller takes back the ticket and tears it up. If you want to change trains, she will give you another larger ticket with a drawing of the tram route, with holes punched in the names of the destination and the transfer station. It is very convenient for passengers to change trains according to the route on the ticket.

We saw a purely Japanese-style street scene in Namba Shinchi. This is one of the bustling centers of Osaka's southern district. The streets are not very wide, and there are mostly Japanese-style houses on both sides. We strolled along the street for a while and walked into the most magnificent building in that area, the "Nankai Takashimaya". The interior layout of this department store is similar to that of the Hankyu Department Store, but the high-priced goods do not seem to be as complete as those of the Hankyu.

In addition to Hankyu and Nankai Takashimaya, there are five other large department stores in Osaka: Mitsukoshi, Daimaru, Jidai, Matsuzakaya, and Takashimaya. None of these big department stores started out as small silk shops (silk and cloth shops). With the annual development of business, the general small shops have suffered a great blow in business? In recent years, small shops have organized associations to resist the power of large department stores through the strength of unity. The department store industry has also formed an association, creating a united front for department stores. When the business competition between the two sides reached a fever pitch, the Osaka Prefectural Office, the City Hall, and the Chamber of Commerce and Industry often came forward to mediate.

The French Government Plans a Draft of a Non-Intervention Agreement, Stipulating an Embargo on Arms to Spain, with Britain Willing to Provide Strong Support 87

(Paris) Regarding the issue of non-intervention in the Spanish civil war, the French government drafted a non-intervention agreement last night and submitted it to the relevant countries. The content stipulates that the signatory countries shall not sell all kinds of military weapons, military and civilian aircraft, and various warships to Spain. The British government has accepted this draft agreement and will support France's position before the governments of the relevant countries. (Havas News Agency, 7th)

(Paris) The government previously sent notes to Britain, Italy, Germany, Russia, the Netherlands, Belgium, Czechoslovakia, and Portugal, advocating the conclusion of an agreement on non-intervention in the Spanish civil war. According to responsible sources, the government will soon issue a second note reiterating the previous proposal and listing specific measures for implementing non-intervention. It is reported that France insists that even contracts already signed should not be fulfilled regarding the prohibition of arms shipments to Spain. So far, most countries have expressed their support for France's first note. Portugal, however, has not yet responded because Foreign Minister Monteiro is currently abroad, and the French ambassador to Portugal, Amié Breleau, will not officially contact the Portuguese government until tomorrow. However, informed sources predict that the Portuguese government will also follow the example of other countries and express its support. It is now known that the British government has begun negotiations on this matter with the Portuguese ambassador to Britain in London. (Havas News Agency, 6th)

French Proposal Gains Support from Seven Countries 88

(Paris) Seven countries have responded, expressing their support for France's note on a joint declaration of non-intervention in Spain, with Italy being one of them. France is currently busy drafting the full text of the agreement. Of the eight countries contacted by France, only Portugal has not yet responded. In total, Britain, Germany, Russia, Italy, Belgium, the Netherlands, and Czechoslovakia agree to non-intervention in the Spanish civil war. It is reported that the agreement currently being drafted aims to prohibit the sale of weapons, bullets, war materials, aircraft, and warships to any party in Spain, Spanish Morocco, or any region under Spanish jurisdiction, and to urge the governments concerned to notify each other of the measures they intend to take to implement the ban on the export of military materials. All types of aircraft are also included in the ban. Once the agreement is drafted, it will be sent to the relevant governments. (Reuters, 7th)

Britain Raises Reservations 89

(London) The British government's views on the draft agreement on non-intervention in Spain proposed by the French government were notified to the French ambassador to London, Corbin, this morning. It is reported that the main difficulty for the British government is the proposal to prohibit the sale of civilian aircraft, as the British government has no power to do so and does not wish to take this special step. The British government believes that the 1925 Geneva Convention is an appropriate basis for the definition of ammunition or war equipment. The Foreign Office only received the French draft yesterday, which was also sent to Britain, Germany, Russia, Italy, Belgium, the Netherlands, and Czechoslovakia. (Reuters, 7th)

Italy and Germany's Attitudes Are Unpredictable 90

(London) Political figures here are quite pessimistic about the prospects for an agreement among the countries concerned on "non-intervention in the Spanish civil war." First, from the Italian perspective, although the Italian government has expressed support in principle for the French proposal, it will raise three questions, requiring France to answer them, namely: (1) Whether expressing sympathy in spirit for one of the warring parties in Spain, such as through demonstrations, newspaper propaganda, donations, and volunteer enlistment, is equivalent to interfering in its civil war; (2) Whether the non-intervention agreement will be universally participated in by the countries concerned, or whether it will only bind the signatory governments, or whether it will apply to the people and private enterprises of each country at the same time; (3) Whether the French government intends to take supervisory measures to ensure that all countries uniformly abide by the non-intervention agreement. Political figures here believe that if Mussolini raises these questions as conditions for Italy's accession to the "non-intervention" agreement, then the French proposal will inevitably fail, and the resulting impact on the international tension will inevitably become more serious, which is truly worrying. Currently, in order to avoid the failure of negotiations, the French government should apply to the Italian government to change its attitude. The British government will also instruct its ambassador to Italy, Sir Drummond, to strongly plead with the Italian government, so as to support France's position. Second, even if Italy is willing to participate in the non-intervention agreement, Germany's attitude is still unknown. It is rumored that Germany will also raise similar questions as conditions for joining the agreement. In addition, the German government has protested to the Spanish government over the shooting of members of the National Socialist Youth Party by Spanish communists. If the Spanish government cannot provide a satisfactory response, Germany and Italy will openly assist the Spanish rebels. If this is the case, then the negotiation of the "non-intervention" agreement will be even more difficult to succeed. According to informed sources here, it is feared that the Spanish government has difficulty in properly protecting the safety of foreigners. In the event that incidents of harming foreigners occur again, then Germany and Italy will inevitably intervene. Third, the Soviet Union is reportedly demanding that several countries immediately cease assisting the Spanish rebels. This demand is clearly aimed at Germany and Italy. In summary, although Britain and France are taking a conciliatory attitude and doing their best to prevent Europe from being divided into two major groups of Fascism and anti-Fascism, it is feared that this attempt will ultimately fail. (Havas News Agency, 6th)

Belgium Willing to Participate and Observe Its Success 91

Brussels The French ambassador, Laroche, visited Foreign Minister Spaak this afternoon to discuss the proposal on non-intervention in the Spanish civil war put forward by the French government. Spaak replied that the Belgian government has in fact prohibited the shipment of arms to Spain, and the government is very willing to participate in the French proposal to observe its success. (Havas News Agency, 6th)

Portugal Objects to Several Points 92

Lisbon, Portugal The French ambassador to Portugal, accompanied by the British Chargé d'Affaires to Portugal, visited Foreign Minister Monteiro this morning and presented the French note on concluding an agreement on non-intervention in the Spanish civil war. Monteiro raised objections to several points contained in the note. (Havas News Agency, 7th)

Development of the Spanish Civil War Deteriorates the International Situation, Causing Great Anxiety Among British and French Figures 93

(London) The daily development of the situation in the Spanish civil war is making the international situation increasingly worse, causing great anxiety among British figures. According to the Daily Herald, the German East Africa Line's steamship "Usaramo" carried 28 bomber aircraft, machine guns, and a batch of ammunition, as well as many pilots and engineers, ostensibly heading to East Africa, but in reality being sent to the Spanish rebel leader, General Franco. After the release of this news, the anxiety of the general public has increased even more. In addition, after four members of the German National Socialist Youth Party in Barcelona, Spain, were executed by Spanish communists a few days ago, the German consul in the city, Köhler, protested to the government of the Autonomous Region of Catalonia. Certain British figures deeply fear that Germany will brazenly occupy the Spanish island of Menorca (belonging to the Balearic Islands) as a guarantee of obtaining a satisfactory response. Also, General Franco seems to intend to prevent Spanish government warships from entering the international neutral port of Tangier. France is unlikely to allow Franco to do as he pleases, thus causing entanglements. All of these are concerns of British figures. (Havas News Agency, 7th)

(Paris) After the government proposed to Britain, Italy, Germany, Russia, the Netherlands, Belgium, Czechoslovakia, and Portugal to conclude an agreement on non-intervention in the Spanish civil war, most of these countries expressed their acceptance of the proposal "in principle." The Ministry of Foreign Affairs is currently working on drafting an implementation plan, but observers believe that the progress of this matter may cause technical difficulties. In addition, news from various capitals is causing unease. Some people are concerned that this external effort is already too late. For example, unofficial sources in Berlin claim that the German government is likely to take the opportunity to either intervene in the port of Mahon on the Spanish island of Menorca (in the Balearic Islands in the Mediterranean) to block the Spanish eastern port of Barcelona, or send troops to land at the port of Ceuta in Spanish Morocco. As for France, the executive committee of the Communist Party has launched a private fundraising campaign to collect funds to support the Spanish "comrades" of the party. At the same time, right-wing nationalists, while acknowledging that the relationship between Italy and Germany and the Spanish rebel leader General Franco is too close, and that France's position in the Mediterranean will be weakened, believe that if the Spanish communists were to win, the harm would be terrifying. Therefore, they advocate that the countries concerned should strictly maintain neutrality on the civil war and not take sides. In addition, news from Moscow claims that although the Soviet government has expressed its acceptance of the French non-intervention proposal in principle, workers everywhere have raised large sums of money to donate to the Madrid government, totaling no less than 36 million francs. As for Italy, the recent aircraft incident in French Algeria, according to the results of the French authorities' investigation, proves that the aircraft indeed belonged to the Italian regular air force and were sent to Spanish Morocco to join the Spanish rebels. Moreover, leftist figures here are widely spreading rumors that when 4,000 troops of the Spanish rebel General Franco crossed the Strait of Gibraltar yesterday on four steamships, several Italian aircraft soared through the sky, escorting them along the way. All of these have already caused fear and doubt. In addition, Italy's response to France's proposal reportedly contains many reservations, which only increases the sense of fear and doubt. (Havas News Agency, 7th)

Large-Scale Arrests of Left-Wing Elements After Greece Implements Dictatorship, Army Remains on High Alert 97

Capital of Yugoslavia According to news from Athens, after the Greek Prime Minister Metaxas dissolved the Chamber of Deputies and implemented a dictatorial regime, all left-wing parties, including the Liberal Party led by former Prime Minister Sophoulis (i.e., the right-wing elements of the former Prime Minister Venizelos's old ministry), expressed their opposition. The government then ordered a large-scale search for opposition elements. Of the Communist Party deputies, a total of 15, except for the leader Stathopoulos, who is in Switzerland and escaped the dragnet, the other 14 were arrested. Liberal Party deputies Gassos and university professor Varotsis were also arrested. Prime Minister Metaxas recently notified the diplomatic envoys of various countries that he had to implement a dictatorial regime because Communist Party members were wantonly carrying out activities that endangered the current political system of the country. As for the military, all members of the Military Association recently declared that they would provide full support to Metaxas, but on the condition that the current positions of officers in the military not be changed. It is reported that the former Minister of the Army, General Papagos, the current Chief of Staff, contributed greatly during the establishment of the dictatorial regime. At this time, the army's vigilance is still extremely strict, with cavalry, gendarmerie, and police densely deployed on the streets of the capital, patrolling back and forth, and all public institutions and strategic locations are guarded by the military. (Havas News Agency, 6th)

The 33rd World Catholic Eucharistic Congress Will Be Held in Manila Next February 98

(Washington) The 33rd World Catholic Eucharistic Congress will be held in Manila, the capital of the Philippines, from February 3 to 7 next year. At that time, ships will gather in Manila Bay. American Catholics have reserved four postal ships, and European ships will also circumnavigate the world, carrying Catholics to the meeting. The 32nd Congress was held last year in the capital of Argentina. For four centuries, the Philippines has been a devout Catholic country, the leader of the Far East. It is said that when Magellan's expedition arrived in the Philippines, the natives of Cebu already had statues of the Santo Niño. The Catholic Church in Manila is also one of the most beautiful Catholic buildings in the world. Therefore, the Catholic authorities believe that Manila is the most appropriate location for the first Congress in the Far East. On February 2 next year, the Pope's representative will arrive in Manila. The Congress will officially open at 5 p.m. the following day. The 4th will be Women's Day, the 5th will be Men's Day, the 6th will be Children's Day, and the 7th will be a Mass service. In mid-April of this year, the Standing Committee of the Congress held a meeting in Paris to prepare everything. The number of representatives from each country is estimated to be 30. As for the number of attendees next year, there is no official estimate at present. In view of the long journey and high cost, it will not be as grand as the previous congresses in Chicago, Dublin, and Buenos Aires, but there will still be representatives from all over the world attending the meeting. (National Telegram, 6th)

Recent News on Fujian Province Facilities: Constructing the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Trunk Road, Promoting Provincial Health, Holding a Special Products Competition 100

Fuzhou Correspondence There are a total of five highways connecting Fujian Province with neighboring provinces: one is from Zhejiang to Fuding in Fujian, which is the first Fujian-Zhejiang trunk road; the second is from Zhejiang to Pucheng in northern Fujian, which is the second Fujian-Zhejiang trunk road; the third is from Jiangxi to Shaowu in northern Fujian, which is the first Fujian-Jiangxi trunk road; the fourth is from Jiangxi to Changting in western Fujian, which is the second Fujian-Jiangxi trunk road; and the fifth is from Guangdong to Yongding in western Fujian, which is the Fujian-Guangdong trunk road. Currently, except for the first Fujian-Zhejiang trunk road, which is still under construction, the other four trunk roads have been completed and opened to traffic. Among them, the second Fujian-Zhejiang trunk road has the longest route, starting from Pucheng on the Zhejiang border, passing through Jianyang, Jian'ou, and connecting to Shaowu, which can lead to Guangze in Jiangxi, then passing through Nanping, Shaxian, Yong'an, and Liancheng, connecting to Changting, which can lead to Ruijin in Jiangxi, and then passing through Longyan and Yongding, which can lead to Dabu in Guangdong. Recently, the Department of Construction plans to build a trunk highway from Minhou, passing through Gutian to Jian'ou, to connect with the second Fujian-Zhejiang trunk road in Pucheng and the first Fujian-Jiangxi trunk road in Shaowu. Currently, the section from Gutian to Jian'ou, which is more than 130 kilometers long, has been surveyed by the surveying team of the National Economic Commission. The Department of Construction has sent engineer Huang Xuan of the Highway General Engineering Office to supervise the construction. The total project cost requires 100,000 yuan, and the provincial government will allocate a portion for application soon. As for the section from Minhou to Gutian, construction will be planned as soon as the terrain survey is clear. After the completion of the project in the future, one can take a long-distance bus from Fuzhou directly to Jiangxi and Zhejiang, and one can also take a long-distance bus from Zhejiang and Jiangxi, passing through Fuzhou directly to Xiamen, Zhangzhou, and other places in southern Fujian. Transportation between the three provinces of Fujian, Jiangxi, and Zhejiang will definitely be more convenient than before. In order to improve the health of the people of Fujian Province, the Fujian Provincial Government has increased the health expenditure in the budget for the 25th year of the Republic by 350,000 yuan, which will be used exclusively for handling provincial health administration, providing medical assistance, and preventing and controlling epidemics. The Third Section of the Department of Civil Affairs will be changed to the Health Section, with Lu Dihuan appointed as the section chief. Under it, there will be three groups: General Affairs, Medicine, and Epidemic Prevention, with Cao Shouli and others appointed as the group leaders. There will also be four technical officers and more than 20 technicians to manage provincial health administration matters. Health offices will be established in Fuzhou and Xiamen to manage public health and epidemic prevention and medical treatment in the two urban areas. They are currently being prepared and will be established soon. In addition, four mobile medical teams will be established to tour various counties, providing medical treatment for the people and providing necessary medicines free of charge. They were organized and established the day before yesterday. Each team will have one director, two doctors, five nurses, and five assistants. The first medical team in the first phase has been designated to depart for Zhenghe, the second medical team to depart for Jiangle, the third medical team to depart for Longyan, and the fourth medical team to depart for Putian, touring various counties. In addition to providing medical treatment for the people, they will also guide the people on health knowledge, so that people can be healthy and increase their working ability.

Fujian Province's various special products, such as tea, wood, paper, dried bamboo shoots, sugar, tobacco leaves, mushrooms, aquatic vegetables, as well as lacquerware, porcelain, umbrellas, and leather cases, used to be very famous. In recent years, due to the lack of improvement in manufacturing methods, sales have decreased day by day, and the local economy has suffered greatly. In order to design to improve special products and promote sales, the Department of Construction held the first provincial special products competition in West Lake Park in Fuzhou last autumn. There were many products from various counties, and the results were very good. Now, in order to continue to urge the progress of various special products, the Department of Construction has decided to hold the second provincial special products competition in Zhangzhou in October of this year. Zhang Yousheng, a technician of the Department of Construction, and Xiao Yijian, the executive director of the National Products Promotion Association, have been sent to prepare for it. As for the Porcelain Industry Exhibition previously planned by the Department of Construction, it has also been decided to merge it with the special products competition. The Dehua County Government will first hold a county-wide porcelain industry competition at the end of July, select good products, and send them to the provincial special products competition for display. The conference has now closed, and there are more than 30 porcelain manufacturing factories participating in the display, with more than 700 kinds of products. After the review, Xu Yuyuan, Su Yunyu, Yan Yili, and more than a dozen other factories are the best, and they have all won super-grade medals. (August 5)

The Zheng Family Uncovers Zheng Xu's Scandal, Zheng Xu Falsely Claims to Be a Descendant of Koxinga, Attempting to Be a Traitor in a Certain Conspiracy, the Fake Bureau is Exposed and He is Arrested in Taiwan 101

Xiamen Correspondence Recently, the Zheng Family Association of Shijing, Nan'an, and the Zheng Family Association of Xiamen uncovered Zheng Xu, who falsely claimed to be a descendant of Koxinga and acted as a traitor. This has had a great impact and happened very quickly. First, not long after the Fujian Incident, there was a Zheng Xu who claimed to be the 12th generation grandson of Koxinga, active in Japanese society. Some Japanese people and the Japanese military regarded him as a treasure and escorted him back to Taiwan to form the "Zheng Family Relics Manifestation Association." On the surface, it was an academic group studying Koxinga's life deeds and words, and a social movement to study Koxinga arose in Japan and Taiwan. Zheng Xu, as a descendant, was ostensibly a central figure, surrounded by a group of people, led by a retired major, who was no less than Zheng Xu's manager. For this reason, the Japanese believed that Koxinga's father, Zhilong, married a Japanese woman from Hirado, Tagawa, who gave birth to Koxinga, and recognized Koxinga as also being of Japanese descent. Koxinga's lifelong achievements were to support the Ming Dynasty and resist the Qing Dynasty, drive out the Dutch, and rule Taiwan for three generations. Taiwan has since been freed from white rule and become a national hero. They took pride in his mother being Japanese and wanted to manifest this. After the association was established, it tried its best to search for Koxinga's cultural relics (a vertical scroll with Koxinga's own handwriting, "Only Heaven is above, and no mountain is equal, raising my head the red sun is near, turning my head white clouds are low," was stolen from the home of a certain Mr. in Anhai, Quanzhou in the winter of the 23rd year of the Republic. Later, it was rumored that someone bought it for 200,000 yuan, which was published in the newspapers. In the summer of the 24th year of the Republic, this scroll was prominently displayed at the Xiamen Taiwan Association Exhibition, and the exhibitor was a Taiwanese named Mr. Wu), and elaborately promoted it. On the one hand, Koxinga's loyalty and integrity are admired by the Chinese people. The people of Fujian, especially those in southern Fujian and Taiwanese who migrated from southern Fujian to Taiwan, have a sacredness to him. Emperor Longwu of the Ming Dynasty gave Koxinga the imperial surname, and Emperor Yongli granted him the title of Prince of Yanping. To this day, the people of Fujian call Koxinga "Imperial Surname Lord" or "Prince of Yanping" instead of his name. The general custom is to directly replace his name with the two characters "Imperial Surname." The Zheng family relics are called "Imperial Surname Tomb," "Imperial Surname Shrine," and "Imperial Surname Well." The depth of their worship can be seen. Therefore, a certain conspiracy wanted to use the psychology of the people of Fujian's worship of Koxinga, and use Koxinga's descendants to carry out a certain separatist movement, with Zheng Xu as the future "South China puppet." Not long after the Fujian Incident, a certain party had a "South China State" conspiracy, but it failed immediately. A certain party then changed to using Zheng Xu. For the past two years, their planning has almost become an open secret and is well known to the people of Fujian. They are also heartbroken that Koxinga has such an unworthy descendant. Koxinga's national consciousness is extremely strong. His support for the Ming Dynasty and resistance to the Qing Dynasty never relied on foreign forces. He dominated southern Fujian, attacked Nanjing in the north, and occupied Taiwan, and never relied on the Japanese pirates who plagued the coastal areas at that time during his lifetime and even for three generations. Recently, the Zheng Family Association of Shijing, Nan'an, Koxinga's hometown, and the Zheng Family General Association of Xiamen jointly published notices in various newspapers in Taiwan, denying that Zheng Xu was a descendant of Koxinga. The notice stated, "After investigation, the Shijing Imperial Surname line has only passed down to the 11th generation, and the 12th generation grandson has not yet been born." This is almost a conclusive proof to refute Zheng Xu as an imposter. After the notice was published, the whole of Taiwan was in an uproar. The Taiwan authorities arrested Zheng Xu and sent him to the military. According to the Zheng family, Zheng Xu is actually from Fuzhou. A few years ago, he passed through Shijing, Nan'an, visited Koxinga's descendants, and paid homage to the Koxinga Ancestral Hall, copying the Koxinga genealogy. At that time, they thought he was worshiping the martyrs and treated him with great courtesy. Later, Xu went to Japan and Taiwan and claimed to be a descendant of Koxinga. The Taiwanese people welcomed him warmly because he talked about the situation of Koxinga's descendants, the ancient relics, ancestral halls, tombs, and the family lineage in an orderly manner, and no one doubted him. Later, Xu was often surrounded by a large number of entourage in Taiwan, opened large hotels, and behaved like an important person. Finally, someone learned that he was colluding with scattered bandits in Fujian, engaging in puppet state activities, and had a certain party background. Therefore, it was widely spread and heard among the Koxinga family members in Shijing, who then exposed his impersonation and issued this notice. The traitor was finally exposed. This move swept away the shadows in the hearts of the people of Fujian and won back a breath for the "Imperial Surname Lord." The matter happened quickly and the impact is not small. (August 6)

Cantonese Merchants Petition for the Abolition of Harsh Taxes 102

Also Petition for the Abolition of Monopoly on Sugar and Native Tobacco Leaves

Guangzhou Correspondence: Since the renovation of the Guangdong Bureau, the government has first declared the prohibition of opium and gambling, and the abolition of all kinds of harsh taxes and miscellaneous levies. The merchants and people are all eagerly awaiting the government to implement the above new policies as soon as possible, in order to relieve the difficulties of merchants and maintain the livelihood of the people of Guangdong. Recently, various merchants have presented to the authorities the harsh and detailed taxes, requesting that they be exempted separately. Those who have appealed daily include: (1) Match merchants. It is found that the match industry in Guangdong Province originally had more than 100 factories. Since the implementation of the unified match tax, each basket of 1,200 boxes of matches must pay a unified tax of three yuan and eight jiao, and a raw material tax of one yuan. The heavy tax on domestically produced matches has led to high costs, making it difficult to compete with foreign matches, resulting in a slump in business. Now the merchants have jointly presented to the authorities, requesting a reduction in the unified tax in order to maintain their business. (2) Coal merchants. Previously, the Special Agricultural Products Tax Bureau levied a special import tax on foreign coal, which not only increased the burden on merchants, but also affected industry. They have again jointly requested the Finance Department to abolish the special coal tax. (3) Special tax on foreign rice. After the Finance Department abolished it, it has recently been levied by the customs. Rice merchants, unaware of the reason, have recently had five rice boats detained by the customs. The Rice Bran Association yesterday sent representatives to negotiate with the Guangdong Customs, and telegraphed the Ministry of Finance to temporarily suspend the levy of foreign rice tax in order to maintain the people's food supply. In addition, various monopoly businesses that compete with the people for profit are close to speculation, raising prices and making people's lives difficult. Those who are currently requesting the abolition of monopolies include: (1) Sugar merchants from various places. Hong Kong sugar merchants sent representatives to the province yesterday to contact local sugar merchants and discuss submitting a petition to the Finance Department to abolish the sugar monopoly. (2) Monopoly on native tobacco leaves. The abuses are serious. Tobacco merchants submitted a petition yesterday requesting its abolition. The petition reads as follows: "(Omitted above) The tobacco tax in Guangdong Province has always been harsh, with a wide variety of tax items. The tobacco tax in Guangdong Province has been monopolized, and the tax rate is 100% of the value, which is twice as high as the original tax. At this time when the people of Guangdong are impoverished, how can they bear the sudden increase in burden? Therefore, on the day of implementation, all tobacco merchants in the province felt the pain of the industry dying. In the past few months, due to poor management, those with inventory are suffering from the indefinite purchase, and those who need it are also suffering from the inability to purchase. To this day, tobacco merchants are heavily taxed and their businesses are exhausted, and they are on the verge of death. The suffering of tobacco farmers is even more countless. The small increase in revenue has caused suffering to the people of Guangdong. Is this the original intention of the government to care for the difficulties of merchants? The merchants are in deep pain and are waiting to be rescued. They dare to present this matter and implore the government to investigate and quickly order the Guangdong-Guangxi-Fujian Unified Tax Bureau to abolish the monopoly on native tobacco leaves on a specific date, follow the central tax system, follow the precedents of various provinces, unify the tax collection, in order to relieve the people's difficulties and care for the merchants' hardships. The telegraph cannot express the anxiety and anticipation. Sincerely, Guangzhou Tobacco Industry Association."

Songjiang: The Exposure of Open Smuggling 104

Li Hengji Rice Shop in Huayang Town, outside the East Gate of this county, has been quite prosperous in business on weekdays. Recently, taking advantage of the smuggling trend, it purchased dozens of packages of fertilizer from Minhang, making huge profits. It then hired a boat to transport them to Songjiang, selling them gradually along the way. When it arrived at the Qiujing Port near Desheng Port, only seven packages remained unsold. This was discovered by Inspector Guo of the Waterborne Provincial Public Security Team stationed there, who suspected that the fertilizer was smuggled and immediately sent police to detain the boat and cargo, and escorted the boatman to the First District Department of Minhang for investigation. It is said that after the incident, the owner of the shop tried to bribe people to intercede, but the First District Department refused his request, and the situation is likely to escalate. Such smuggling activities should be severely punished.

Taicang: A Righteous Gang Fights Robbers and Dies 105

Hu Yimao Wine Shop in Yuewang Market, the Fifth District of the county, has two stores, east and west. Hu Youhe, the owner of the east store, had a slight surplus of money, which had long been coveted by bandits. Fortunately, the owner took strict precautions and nothing had happened. At midnight on the 5th, during a torrential rain, seven robbers suddenly came. Two bandits were on the lookout outside, and the remaining bandits, unable to enter the room, climbed onto the roof of the backyard and broke through the roof. Zhang Laogen, the wine clerk, had served in the shop since childhood, was unusually strong, had a lot of integrity, and was deeply loved by the owner. He was the first to be awakened and looked out to see a figure. He hid in the dark to observe his actions and saw the bandits trying to enter the owner's bedroom. He bravely stepped forward and hugged the leader of the bandits around the waist, preventing him from moving. Seeing this, the remaining bandits fired two shots at Zhang, one hitting his waist and one hitting his leg. He still didn't feel anything and fought bravely. Because he was outnumbered, he broke free and shouted, running to the street before falling to the ground and dying. After Zhang went out, the robbers searched and looted, taking the stolen goods and heading southeast. After the incident, it was found that more than 500 yuan of jewelry and silver dollars had been robbed. The county was immediately notified to investigate and arrest the robbers. The body was taken to the scene for examination by Examiner Shen Cheng and the forensic officer. After being properly dressed, it was handed over to the family for burial.

Each district, township, and town in this county will hold a citizens' oath registration, which must be completed by the 15th of this month. Training Monks and Taoists Throughout the County 109

County Magistrate Long Tiyao, in order to enable Buddhists throughout the county to cope with extraordinary times, has specially organized a first-aid training class for monks. He ordered Wei Zhiwen of the Wuxi Branch of the Chinese Buddhist Association to be responsible for the preparation and to formulate a simple outline and training program. There are more than 600 temples in the urban and rural areas of this county. All monks and Taoists between the ages of 18 and 45 must be transferred to the city for training. The training location is borrowed from the Central Elementary School. The training subjects include Buddhism, Party principles, medicine, hygiene, first aid, nursing, air defense, poison gas prevention, etc. In the first phase, the abbots of each temple will be trained first, followed by the guest teachers of each temple. The training expenses will be shared by each temple. Master Chao Yi was appointed as the director and Wei Zhiwen as the deputy director. Training is scheduled to begin after the 15th of this month.

Jiangyin: Tianzhang Bankrupt and Debt Sharing 110

Tian Zhang Silk and Cloth Shop on East Street, since the owner Gu Muyong ran away, has been declared bankrupt and liquidated. Shen Ben, the county commissioner, and the creditors checked the goods and financial accounts, which has been completed. A meeting was held at the County Chamber of Commerce on the 5th. Commissioner Shen Cheng reported that Tian Zhang's entire account showed a loss of 36,016 yuan, 1 jiao, and 7.2 li in deposit accounts, and 9,208 yuan, 2 jiao, 7.2 li in guest accounts, for a total loss of 45,498 yuan, 9 jiao, and 7.4 li. The goods found were estimated to be worth 12,520 yuan and 5 jiao. Later, it was discovered in the kitchen that hidden cloth was estimated to be worth 234 yuan and 6 jiao, and miscellaneous household items were estimated to be worth 700 yuan. Cash held at the county office not allowed to be transferred amounted to 1,000 yuan, for a total of 14,565 yuan and 1 jiao. It was decided that 500 yuan would be deducted for various expenses, and the remaining 14,065 yuan and 1 jiao would be distributed according to 30% of the shop's debt. There are still house rentals and debts owed by people, which will be distributed after the exact amount is checked. Debts owed by people should be collected by the shop's partners Ye Fusheng, Han Shenqing, and Wu Tongkai before the Mid-Autumn Festival. If they are overdue, a list will be submitted to the county for collection.

Telegraph Courier Forges Telegrams 112

Ding Zhusan, a telegraph courier at the Nantong Telegraph Bureau, stole blank telegram paper, forged telegrams, and stole stamps to send to well-known merchants in remote towns such as Sanyu and Jugang, defrauding them of delivery fees. Later, the recipients of the telegrams read the telegrams and were confused. They reported to the telegraph bureau for inquiry and found out that they had been deceived. In addition to the bureau refunding the defrauded delivery fees, Ding Zhusan was sent to the Public Security Bureau. A telegram was sent to the Ministry of Communications for instructions. A reply was received from the Telegraph Department, ordering Ding to be transferred to the court. After interrogation by the procuratorate, he was detained.

Hangzhou: Reorganizing the Qiantang River Wharf 115

The Meihua Chun on the north and south banks of the Qiantang River Ferry was previously eaten by saltwater worms and eroded by tides, causing them to break, which hindered the safety of the wharf. Due to the provincial treasury's deficit, it could not be held in advance. Now that the Hangzhou-Linhai Highway has been jointly operated, the relationship between the north and south banks of the Qiantang River Wharf and the cross-river passengers is more important than before. The Anti-Smuggling Federation Begins Work, Submitting a Report to the Party and Government in Beijing for Record 119

The National Anti-Smuggling Federation of Chambers of Commerce of Various Provinces and Cities, which was resolved to be organized at the joint meeting of chambers of commerce of various provinces and cities, is now actively working. Yesterday, the process of organization was reported to the Central Party Headquarters, the Ministry of Finance, the Shanghai Municipal Party Headquarters, and the Municipal Government for record. The original text reads, "A report is submitted for the organization of the National Anti-Smuggling Federation, requesting review and record. Since the smuggling problem in North China occurred, it has damaged our national administration, harmed our national tax revenue, and the impact has been profound and significant. The endangered industry and commerce have been further pushed to the brink of bankruptcy by this attack. Fortunately, the central government has promulgated special laws and regulations to strictly investigate and punish them, and to encourage industrial and commercial organizations to report each other in order to achieve cooperation. Our industry and commerce have a vital stake in this matter, and we should follow the central government's intentions and strive to save ourselves. In addition to the chambers of commerce of various provinces, cities, and counties separately organizing anti-smuggling associations to assist the government in investigating and punishing tax-evading smuggled goods, and to maintain the legitimate sales of goods, the joint meeting of chambers of commerce of 21 provinces, cities, and counties has resolved to organize the National Anti-Smuggling Federation of Chambers of Commerce of Various Provinces and Cities in order to concentrate forces and unify steps. Commissioners have been elected, and the establishment has been officially announced, with an office located in the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce. The organizational outline and the list of commissioners are hereby submitted for review, requesting approval for record in order to facilitate the work, which would be greatly appreciated."

Shanghai Goods Exported to the United States in July and the First Seven Months 120

Increased Compared to the Same Period Last Year

According to statistics released by the U.S. Consulate General in Shanghai, Shanghai's exports to the United States and its territories in July increased compared to the same month last year. Shanghai's exports to the United States in the first seven months of this year totaled US$11,073,669, an increase of US$2 million compared to the same period last year. There are three main categories of trade: (1) cattle and sheep hides and leather goods, (2) inedible plant products and oils, and (3) textiles. In the first category, goatskins and lambskins totaled US$1,377,849, and gray squirrel skins totaled US$1,118,938. In the second category, sesame seeds totaled US$1,501,870, and tung oil totaled US$1,295,030. In the third category, textiles totaled US$3,197,286, including waste cotton accounting for US$305,915, embroidery accounting for US$970,966, and straw hats accounting for US$329,008. Exports to the Philippines in the seven months totaled US$689,373, and exports to Hawaii totaled US$32,739.

The 6% British Gold Custody Committee Ends and is Dissolved 121

The Yuehan Railway is Completed

Documents Designated for Agency Takeover

Dagong News Agency reports that in order to complete the Zhushao section of the Yuehan Railway, the Ministry of Railways, together with the Ministry of Finance, issued 6% British Gold Gengkuan Public Bonds in the 23rd year of the Republic of China. At that time, in accordance with the regulations of the public bonds, it jointly organized the "6% British Gold Gengkuan Public Bond Debt Custody Committee" with relevant agencies such as the Ministry of Finance, the Auditing Department, and the Sino-British Gengkuan Board of Trustees to handle the custody and disbursement of all debt funds. The committee has been established since July of the 23rd year and has been in operation for two years. According to reports from Dagong News Agency reporters, the total amount of debt funds received by the committee over the past two years has reached £1,350,000, which has been allocated to the Yuehan Railway Bureau for the construction of the Zhushao section. Now that the Ministry of Railways has found that the construction of the section has been completed and the debt funds held by the committee have been fully disbursed, in accordance with Article 8 of the committee's organizational regulations, "dissolution on the date when the debt funds are fully disbursed," the committee will be closed and dissolved. All documents, files, official seals, and account books of the committee have been taken over and kept by personnel sent by the Ministry of Railways together with the receiving agency designated by the Ministry of Finance. After being ordered to handle the closure, the committee has reported to the Ministry of Railways for record and has sent separate letters to all parties.

Change in the Principles of Property Re-Mortgage Rights 122

Supported by the Banking and Money Industries

Consultation on Detailed Measures

The Shanghai Real Estate Industry Association, in view of the fact that the real estate industry is the most important asset in the market, but the real estate industry has been affected by the global economic recession for many years, with prices plummeting and transactions disappearing, resulting in a lack of assets, in order to increase the assets in the market and save the real estate industry, has resolved to jointly request the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Finance, to change the property re-mortgage rights. For example, if A mortgages the property to B, and then B re-mortgages it to C, if B is liquidated, C has no priority right. Now, the request is to still give C priority right. The Banking Association has approved the request to change the re-mortgage rights in principle. Yesterday, it replied to the Real Estate Industry Association, but the detailed measures must be agreed upon by the three organizations in a joint meeting. After research, the Money Industry Association also approved the principle, but it must be passed by the ten-day executive committee before replying to the Real Estate Industry Association.

The Jinghu Railway Clears Debt for Purchasing Cars

Contract Cancellation 123

Notice to the Sino-British Company to Invalidate

In June of the 18th year of the Republic of China, the Jinghu Railway and the Sino-British Banking Company signed a contract for purchasing cars on credit. Interest was charged at 8% per week from the date of payment for the purchase of materials. The total credit amounted to £161,574, 13 shillings, and 2 pence. Under the supervision of the Ministry of Railways, the railway was required to deposit a special debt repayment reserve monthly from its operating income. Since the funds have been repaid successively, the credit has been fully repaid as of recently. The railway bureau has formally notified the Sino-British Company to cancel and invalidate the previously signed contract for purchasing cars on credit.

Our Prohibition on the Export of Waste Cotton, Japanese Merchants Oppose Unreasonably 125

Shen Shi News Agency reports that our country's annual waste cotton exports reach more than 10 million yuan. The United Kingdom, the United States, Germany, Japan, France, Italy, and other countries purchase large quantities. This item is used to manufacture gunpowder raw materials. Recently, the Jianghai Customs issued an order prohibiting exports, because our country needs to use waste cotton to help refugees who have no clothes to cover their bodies. Since the issuance of the order, British, American, and German merchants have raised no objections, but the Japanese merchants residing in Shanghai, the people of our friendly nation, have unreasonably opposed it in a group, which is very intense.

The Ministry of Communications' Zhabei Long-Distance Telephone Station Opens for Calls at Midnight Today, Temporarily Using 20 Pairs of Sending and Receiving Relay Lines, and the Transmission Wave Amplifying Machine is Activated at the Same Time 126

Dagong News Agency reports that the Zhabei Long-Distance New Telephone Station built by the Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Communications is located south of Yongxing Road on Yuyingtang Road in Zhabei, adjacent to the east of the Zhabei Branch of the Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Communications. The land area is 0.56 mu, and a three-story Western-style building with cement and steel frames has been built. The ground floor is divided into (1) a power generation room, (2) an electrical porcelain room, (3) an amplifier room, and (4) a repair room. The front part of the middle floor is the international wireless telephone room, and the back part is the long-distance telephone exchange. The upper floor is a dormitory. The construction is quite novel and beautiful.

Long-Distance Lines

The materials and machines used in the station were ordered from the United Kingdom. There are 40 pairs of long-distance telephone sending and receiving relays. 20 pairs will be activated temporarily, distributing them to various places along the Jinghu and Huhangyong routes, and for the long-distance telephones that have been opened in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces. The remaining 20 pairs will be used after the completion of the Nine Provinces Telephone.

Midnight Calls

Since the completion of the new station building, the Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Communications has been installing various machines one after another, which has been completed. Since August 4th, continuous test calls have been made with various places, and the results have been excellent. Therefore, it has been decided to officially open for calls at 12:30 AM today. At that time, Director Xu Xueyu, Chief Engineer Yu Bingjian, together with the heads of the Long-Distance Department and the Zhabei Branch, Fan and Zhu, will supervise the staff and preside over the call affairs.

Booster Amplification

Long-distance telephones, whenever there is wind and rain, sometimes encounter obstacles due to the distance, and the sound waves are considerably affected. Now, in order to boost the radio waves and increase the sound waves, the station has specially attached a booster amplification machine. Regardless of the distance, it can increase the sound waves at any time, which is a special feature of our country's long-distance telephone equipment. The machine will also be activated at the same time when the calls are made.

Rong Zongjing Speaks on Using Cotton and Iron to Save the Nation: Smuggling Runs Rampant, Threatening the Yarn Industry; The National Economic Council Plans Relief Measures 127

The national yarn industry is increasingly threatened by the encroachment of foreign yarn. Major figures in the yarn industry are exchanging opinions on how to survive. A reporter from the Industrial News visited Rong Zongjing, a leading figure in the yarn industry, to inquire about his views. He replied that China's yarn industry has a long history. When Mr. Zhang Jian of Nantong served as Minister of Industry, he loudly advocated using cotton and iron to save the nation. Later, Mr. Nie Yuntai also actively advocated revitalizing the textile industry to save China. He himself (Rong Zongjing referring to himself) also absolutely advocated implementing the plan of using cotton and iron to save the nation. However, times have changed, and the market has gradually become depressed. Production and sales are not balanced, and supply even exceeds demand. The reason is the influence of foreign yarn dumping. In recent years, the business of Chinese yarn factories has declined day by day, and now they are almost completely unable to maintain themselves. Currently, smuggling is rampant, and the yarn industry is on the verge of collapse. Although the authorities of various factories are exchanging opinions on how to save the situation, it is unpredictable whether they can be realized. Without concrete measures, shouting for self-rescue will be in vain. In recent days, Chen Guangfu, chairman of the Cotton Industry Control Committee of the National Economic Council, has also convened several meetings. A concrete plan to rescue the yarn industry has been largely developed. It is said that after future consultations are finalized, it will be submitted to Minister Song Ziwen to request the Ministries of Finance and Industry to discuss implementation.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Replies: Measures for Implementing Industry Regulations 130

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce replied to the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs yesterday, stating that it was in response to the Bureau's instruction No. 3038 of the General Office on the fifth of this month, requesting that the various industry guilds be instructed to prepare detailed plans for the implementation of industry regulations and effective handling, for reference. The Chamber stated that the nature of industry regulations is a commercial agreement jointly resolved by members of the same industry, which is no different from a contract jointly entered into by a majority of parties involved in a commercial relationship. In the proposal to discuss and amend the Law on Industry Guilds at the joint meeting of provincial and municipal chambers of commerce on July 20, there was a proposal to add a clause after Article 4 of the current Law on Industry Guilds, stating that industry guilds should, in addition to their articles of association, formulate industry regulations to standardize prices, limit production, and define quality by consensus of the industry. These industry regulations are considered part of the guild's articles of association, and those who violate them may be subject to fines or confiscation of the goods in violation. When necessary, they may also be sued in the competent court and executed in accordance with civil litigation procedures. According to the above proposal, in areas where administrative power is complete, those who violate industry regulations can be subject to administrative penalties, such as fines or confiscation of goods in violation. In special circumstances, such as within the Shanghai Concessions, they can also sue for breach of commercial contract and ask the court to order the violator to compensate for losses. It seems that all situations can be taken care of, and there will be no feeling of difficulty in implementation. It has been resolved that the various chambers of commerce attending the joint meeting will submit the proposal to the Legislative Yuan and the Ministry of Industry in the name of the chamber of commerce. This opinion represents the common will of the chambers of commerce in various places and seems to be sufficient to represent the general opinion of the various industry guilds. In response to the previous order, a document is hereby prepared and submitted, requesting the Bureau to review and approve it for implementation, as it is in the public interest.

Zhejiang Cocoon Industry Association Submits to the Zhejiang Provincial Government: Return Sample Cocoons for Trial Reeling 136

Please Pay According to Market Price as Usual

Otherwise, the Sample Cocoons Should Be Returned

The Zhejiang Cocoon Industry Association Joint Association, located on Avenue Edward VII, Lianzhuli, this port, submitted a document to the Zhejiang Provincial Government requesting the return of sample cocoons for trial reeling, stating: "Regarding the request, according to the cocoon merchants who purchased cocoons in the spring period, they have complained to the association that the Cocoon and Silk Control Committee of this term, believing that the cocoon merchants who purchased fresh cocoons did not reach the central price, extracted sample cocoons for trial reeling to determine the quality of the cocoons. According to the merchants' usual practice, these sample cocoons must be compensated at the market price. Now, the Control Committee has taken a considerable number of sample cocoons from the cocoon merchants, and it does not seem appropriate to take people's goods without compensation. Therefore, we request that the sample cocoons and sample silks taken be returned. According to this, it is found that in the market, whether the purchase of dry cocoons is successful or not, the sample cocoons should be priced at the market price. Now, the Cocoon and Silk Control Committee does not price the sample cocoons taken from the cocoon shops at the market price due to the trial reeling, and the sample cocoons should also be returned to ensure fairness and avoid criticism. Based on the previous situation, we hereby submit this request to your government for review and approval to instruct implementation, as it is in the public interest. Sincerely submitted to the Zhejiang Provincial Government."

Employees of the China Credit Information Bureau Went on Strike Yesterday Morning: Employees Put Forward Demands 140

According to the Dagong News Agency, since the resignation of Chairman Zhang Naiqi of the China Credit Information Bureau on Yuanmingyuan Road in this port, the board of directors elected Zhu Yangchen as the new chairman. After Chairman Zhu took office, he dismissed three employees, causing a reaction from all colleagues. Yesterday morning at 9:00 AM, all employees and printing workers suddenly united and declared a strike. The details are recorded as follows:

Contents of the Bureau

The bureau was established four years ago and is jointly operated by more than 20 banks, including the Bank of China and the Bank of Communications. It specializes in credit investigations. It is divided into seven sections: investigation, documentation, information, general affairs, line name, printing, and the secretary's office. Zhang Naiqi served as chairman, and Pan Yangyao served as manager (but Pan has resigned and has not been replaced). There are more than 80 employees and printing workers in the bureau. Through four years of effort, the business has gradually developed, and the finances have become independent. Branch offices have also been added in Hankou and Tianjin. Since Mr. Zhang resigned as chairman last month, the board of directors decided to appoint Zhu Yangchen, director of the Investigation Department of the Bank of China, as chairman to be responsible for all affairs of the bureau.

Cause of the Strike

After Chairman Zhu took office, he transferred Ge Shiliang, the original secretary, to be the director of the Information Department. Zhu Longyi, secretary of the China Credit Association, was appointed to concurrently replace Ge. Li Baimeng, the director of the Information Department, was transferred to be a clerk in the Documentation Department. Three other employees in the Documentation and Investigation Departments were dismissed, causing dissatisfaction among all colleagues. They negotiated with Chairman Zhu. Mr. Zhu admitted that his actions were inappropriate, and Zhang Naiqi also came forward to mediate. However, as of yesterday, because Mr. Zhu still failed to implement the reconciliation plan, all employees, including the printing workers and tea servants, jointly went on strike at 9:00 AM yesterday.

Situation of the Workers

A reporter specially visited the foreman of the printing department yesterday. According to him, the workers of the bureau are required to work from 9:00 AM to 8:00 PM every day, but in reality, the working hours must be extended to 12:00 AM or 1:00 AM to complete the work. The monthly salary is at most 15 yuan, and the meals on Sundays and holidays are paid for by themselves. The work limited each day must complete 50 pages, otherwise a day's salary will be deducted. A few days ago, three or four workers had already left because they could not maintain their livelihoods. There are currently 10 workers in total, and they all feel that the new chairman's treatment is harsh. Therefore, they also sympathize with the employees and take a consistent action.

Demands Put Forward

The demands of the employees and workers of the bureau were put forward to the new chairman by Li Baimeng and Yang Jialun, the directors of the Information Department and the General Affairs Department, respectively. The demands of the employees are: (1) Demand to ensure the safety of their positions; (2) Withdraw the order to dismiss employees; (3) Request the government authorities to thoroughly investigate the bad elements within the bureau; (4) Strictly punish employees who sow discord; (5) Restore the position of secretary. The demands of the workers are: (1) Increase wages to maintain livelihoods; (2) Reduce working hours; (3) Subsidize meal expenses on holidays; (4) Cannot be arbitrarily dismissed without cause.

Welcoming the Spirit Method

The method for welcoming the spirit is as follows: (1) Ask the Municipal Party Headquarters to issue a notice to all party members and mass organizations to participate in welcoming the spirit, and order all levels of party headquarters to fly the flag at half-mast for one day when Mr. Wu Xingya's coffin arrives in the city to express condolences; (2) Ask the Municipal Government to issue a notice to its affiliated agencies to send personnel to participate in welcoming the spirit, and order all agencies and the public in the city to fly the flag at half-mast for one day when Mr. Wu Xingya's coffin arrives; (3) Ask the Garrison Command and the Municipal Public Security Bureau to send a band to participate in welcoming the spirit; (4) This committee will send personnel to lead the spirit moving ceremony, prepare various sacrificial offerings, designate all standing committee members as chief officiants, directors of each group as assistant officiants, and all committee members to participate in the memorial service; (6) Ask the Social Affairs Bureau to issue a notice to all social organizations to send personnel to participate in welcoming the spirit.

Public Memorial Service Procedure

The date and location of the public memorial service will be decided temporarily. The procedure for the public memorial service is as follows: on the first morning, a public memorial service will be held by party and government agencies; in the afternoon, a public memorial service will be held by merchant groups; on the second morning, a public memorial service will be held by worker groups; in the afternoon, a public memorial service will be held by youth and cultural groups; on the third morning, a public memorial service will be held by social groups; and in the afternoon, a public memorial service will be held by farmer groups.

Preparations for Memorial Service

Tong Xingbai, Zhang Xiaotong, Du Yuesheng, Wang Xiaolai, Xu Yefu, Wu Huanru, Wang Shaozhai, Li Dachao, Zhou Xuexiang, Yu Zhenhui, Zheng Jie, etc. were appointed as members of the preparatory committee, and Tong Xingbai was appointed as convener.

Chinese Tea Can Be Expected to Dominate the International Market 147

Black Tea Exports Account for Two-Fifths

Three Major Reforms as Reasons for Improvement

According to Dagong News, this year's tea trade with foreign countries has greatly increased in price and exports are booming due to major reforms in quality and marketing. Purchases are made by countries such as England, America, France, Germany, the Netherlands, and Morocco. Green tea accounts for the majority of exports, with black tea only accounting for two-fifths of green tea, because the demand for black tea is not as widespread as that for green tea. There are three reasons for the sudden improvement in exports: (1) Since China has sought to develop black tea, in addition to implementing unified marketing, the National Economic Council has also jointly established experimental farms with tea merchants in Anhui and Jiangxi to promote scientific roasting methods, and the quality has been improving day by day, surpassing Indian and Ceylon tea. (2) Although countries such as England, Russia, France, and the United States have promoted tea planting, it is difficult to achieve results due to unsuitable land. (3) The production of Indian, Javanese, and Ceylon teas, which compete with Chinese tea in the international market, has sharply decreased in recent years, so Chinese tea has taken advantage of the situation. Therefore, general European and African tea merchants believe that if Chinese tea can strive to improve and not slacken, it can dominate the international tea market in a few years.

New Purchases for the Municipal Zoo Fierce Tigers and Giant Elephants Arrive in Shanghai One Male Tiger and a Pair of Elephants Open for Exhibition in the Garden Today 151

The Municipal Zoo on Wenmiao Road was established in August of the 22nd year of the Republic of China and has been open for three years. On weekdays, there are always more than 3,000 visitors. On weekends and holidays, the number of visitors often exceeds 10,000. The zoo recently purchased a fierce Indian tiger and a pair of Siamese giant elephants, which arrived in Shanghai yesterday and will be open for exhibition today. The details are recorded as follows:

Indian Tiger

The zoo originally had a tiger, which died of pulmonary tuberculosis in the spring of this year. Since then, it has been trying to solicit purchases everywhere, but it is difficult to obtain live tigers. After a long time, there were no responding goods. This time, the Dingxingtai Animal Trading Company in this city undertook the purchase and obtained a male Indian tiger in Singapore. It is three years old and weighs 120 kilograms. It arrived in port yesterday at noon on the Bainxianer Wheel. The tiger pen in the park had been disinfected with a flamethrower in advance to ensure safety. The tiger was transported to the park at 6:00 PM and will be open for exhibition today.

Siamese Giant Elephants

The zoo also ordered a pair of Siamese giant elephants from an animal merchant in Singapore. They are five feet tall, three years old, strong, and have a loud voice. They arrived in the park at the same time as the tiger. The park is now reporting to the Municipal Government to send personnel for acceptance. The park has built a small garden specifically for the giant elephants to bathe and exercise. The giant elephants bathing are quite interesting, it is said.

Customs Seizes Smuggled Artificial Silk One Person Arrested, Two Accomplices Escape 154

At 5:00 AM on the 31st of last month, a man named Zhang Ahu rented a gasoline boat from the Jiu Jiang Road Shihe Ferry Company and sailed to the vicinity of the fish market to wait. At about 6:00 AM, the Japanese ship Fengtian Maru arrived. Zhang instructed the boatman to bring the boat close to the side of the ship. Suddenly, two packages of artificial silk were thrown down from the ship. Just as they were about to escape, they were spotted by the Customs patrol boat Guanwei, which took the people, boat, and silk to the Water Police Station. The artificial silk weighed 90.71 kilograms and was worth 130 yuan. It was confirmed to be smuggled goods evading taxes. The police chief believed that this was the first time that the Customs had seized smuggled goods. In order to investigate the smuggling organization, Zhang Ahu was interrogated in detail. According to Zhang's confession, there were also two accomplices, Zhu Agui and Sun Guixing, who were hiding at No. 48 Jingfu Lane, Beikaier Road, Hongkou, and No. 152 Pingliang Road. Detectives were sent to search for them, but they had already fled upon hearing the news. As of yesterday, there were still no clues. The criminal Zhang was formally sent to the District Court for interrogation, the smuggled silk was confiscated by the Customs, and the boat used for smuggling was detained, awaiting the Customs' disposal in accordance with the law.

The China National Goods Cigarette Maintenance Association, after announcing its establishment last year, has been actively working without reservation. In addition to holding exhibitions to expand publicity, it also invited people from all walks of life to hold a publicity conference at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce on the afternoon of August 8th, resolving to designate August 8th as the National Goods Cigarette Commemorative Day, in order to awaken compatriots to jointly maintain it. Now that the one-year term of the association is approaching, it held the "August 8th Festival" anniversary yesterday at the Lao Jin Long Restaurant. Attendees included Yuan Ludeng, Shen Weiting, Bao Gengsheng, Jing Yimeng, Wu Linzhi, Sun Daosheng, Wang Junzhi, etc. Mr. Yuan Ludeng chaired the meeting and delivered a commemorative speech on behalf of all the committee members. Next, the meeting discussed association affairs, and finally, a dinner was held before dispersing. The commemorative speech is recorded as follows: "Time flies, and today is another auspicious day for the August 8th anniversary. How delightful! However, in the past year, although the business of domestic cigarettes has been extensively promoted and fully maintained by our association, the business situation has ultimately been subject to environmental control, making it difficult to reverse its decline. This is truly regrettable for the members of our association, but there is nothing we can do. Since recent years, the country's progress has been difficult, the countryside is on the verge of crisis, and the social economy has suffered exhaustion, resulting in a decrease in purchasing power, which has greatly impacted the cigarette business. Moreover, our Chinese factories have only recently emerged, with weak financial resources, working diligently day and night, still fearing to fall behind. On the other hand, foreign cigarette factories have a long history and possess strong forces, watching fiercely and swallowing like whales, rising up to compete, which is a formidable enemy for our Chinese factories. It is difficult to seek maximum development. Recently, due to cigarette smuggling from a certain country, smuggled cigarettes are flooding various places, causing hand-cranked and handmade tax-evading cigarettes to flourish like wildfire, spreading daily and encroaching on the sales figures of cigarette factories, which is alarming. Chinese factories are suffering from these multiple influences, so how can business not decline day by day? This is also what the members of our association lament today. From now on, we earnestly hope that compatriots across the country will uphold their fearless spirit and rise up to promote national goods. Then this August 8th festival will also be commemorated without limit. It will be fortunate for the country and fortunate for our association."
